1910s : ai yer git goin nothin talkin somethin knowed seein tellin workin comin doin dat em thinkin gettin mornin dere feelin fer s'pose cryin runnin tryin lettin lookin ag'in gits gittin agin mebbe ridin ef thar gon outa waitin watchin nuthin bein sayin jist critter heerd yit kinda foller worryin takin a-goin settin livin havin wantin whar foolin knowin lyin anythin leavin makin yo willin i'se givin turnin druv hidin fightin eatin jes shootin mawnin lak dey sech outen afore wid pickin callin huntin playin puttin thout jest yourn stickin feller leetle yerself roun ketched 'm thet yuh reckon askin hev
1920s : ai goin git yer nothin somethin talkin tellin seein doin thinkin knowed em dat workin comin gettin s'pose runnin ag'in dere cryin mornin tryin feelin mebbe nuthin fer lettin gon lookin watchin worryin a-goin ridin gits bein gittin foller mawnin kinda waitin takin agin thar leavin havin ef whar outa knowin willin yit foolin anythin critter heerd sayin livin jist fightin hidin playin makin wantin lyin settin yuh puttin druv ketched jes i'se pickin outen killin dey shootin yo drinkin eatin leetle hearin wid uns afore bout dyin askin givin turnin evenin lak sittin reg'lar yourn jest walkin callin thout
